4,753,204,941,224,195091,8449,"R4|||||||19|80|YCN|0|0|X|X|0|||0|0|4|0|0||||","F=Arial|T=T","Stump care~UMBILICAL STUMP CARE~Parents advised that umbilical stump will detach on its own in approximately 7-10 days. Counseled that the site should be kept clean and dry, and that there is no need to clean it with alcohol (this can actually prolong the process). Discussed that the infant should not be bathed or immersed in water until the umbilical stump is healed and a minimum of 24 hrs have have passed since detaching. An umbilical stump that is not drying out or falling off by 2 weeks of age should be evaluated by a physician. Parents stated understanding.~ ~ "
